## Status: PARTIAL KEEP - Stage 4a right Householder workspace, Stage 4d fused rank-k far update, and Stage 4h thin-factor reflector replay shipped; z65tz continues via packed panel buffers or two-stage communication-avoiding bidiagonalization

## Missions
1. Contract and profile gate: confirm a full-rank rectangular `lstsq`/`pinv` target with RCH baseline/profile evidence and reserve the linalg surface.
2. Alien primitive selection: route the measured bottleneck through blocked bidiagonalization / numerical-linear-algebra primitives and reject behavior-changing shortcuts.
3. One-lever implementation: make at most one narrow source change that preserves solution, rank, singular-value ordering/length, residual policy, certificates, errors, and RNG absence.
4. Proof and rebench: golden SHA, focused tests, crate-scoped RCH validation, UBS, and same-worker before/after benchmark.
5. Closeout and reprofile: keep only Score >= 2.0, close `frankenscipy-vgs9h`, sync beads, commit, push `main` and `main:master`, then re-run `br ready --json`.

## Completed Passes

### Pass 1 - frankenscipy-127pc SpMM fused chunk execution
- Bead: `frankenscipy-127pc`
- Lever: fused each work-balanced SpMM chunk's symbolic count and numeric fill inside the same worker. This removes the second scoped thread fanout while preserving the existing row-local numeric kernel.
- Baseline: RCH `ts2`, `sparse_spmm/2000x2000_d1/2000`, median `13.405 ms`, interval `[13.333 ms, 13.481 ms]`.
- After: RCH `ts2`, median `11.632 ms`, interval `[11.417 ms, 11.838 ms]`.
- Delta: `13.2%` faster by median.
- Isomorphism: row/range order, A traversal, B encounter order, reverse first-seen output order, FP accumulation order, zero elision, sorted metadata, and RNG absence preserved because `spmm_row_chunk` remains the numeric path; `debug_assert_eq!` keeps numeric counts tied to symbolic counts.
